  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_34d94cba-32e3-431d-a2a9-fe154ba68b41'

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/35546107" />
    <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"><img alt=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1403239075p2/1570669.jpg" /></a>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/35546107?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"> Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780312984823" href="/book/show/84140.Night_Embrace">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=bad-boy-rake-or-rogue">bad-boy-rake-or-rogue</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=scary-sexy-cool-dangerous-hero">scary-sexy-cool-dangerous-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=vampire">vampire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=owned-copy">owned-copy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer35546107" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5136197137699782380">I wasn't crazy about this DH book like the other ones because, gasp, I think there is too much sex in this book. The sex scenes get to the point where you're skimming because you want to get back to the story. I realize that fundamentally, Sunshine and Talon are very sexual beings. No issue there. Some people are. But after a while I didn't really need to read more scenes with them being sexual. I just got old and distracting from the plot and Kenyon's phenomenal storytelling.<br/><br/>Talon's backstory w</span>
  <span id="freeText5136197137699782380" style="display:none">I wasn't crazy about this DH book like the other ones because, gasp, I think there is too much sex in this book. The sex scenes get to the point where you're skimming because you want to get back to the story. I realize that fundamentally, Sunshine and Talon are very sexual beings. No issue there. Some people are. But after a while I didn't really need to read more scenes with them being sexual. I just got old and distracting from the plot and Kenyon's phenomenal storytelling.<br /><br />Talon's backstory was very interesting, and I wanted to read more about that than him and Sunshine shagging. He's half-pagan and half-Christian with a Celtic heritage. He lost his whole village, partly through some of his actions. His past is very tragic and sets the tone for his future. Now he's a Dark Hunter who kills Daemons and shags as many beautiful women as he can to while away his time. Okay. Some readers probably find that sexy. I really didn't. His backstory worked tremendously well, but I didn't love present aspects of Talon's character. As for Sunshine, I just didn't find her that interesting. She came off as kind of a sleazy, hippieish, biker groupie chick. I'm not saying that's bad, but she didn't really intrigue me. She was nice and sweet, but just not a heroine that I got involved with as a reader. But I do have to say, they were very much kindred souls, and I am very glad they found their happy ending together.<br /><br />The best aspects of this book were the secondary characters and the intricate world that Sherrilyn Kenyon has created with her Dark Hunter books. I can never get enough of it. She's a marvelous writer, and does a great job at taking ancient history and the myths and building a modern storyline around this foundation. The standout character in this book for me is Zarek. He got my attention from the get-go. Probably because I really like the dark, conflicted, antiheroes. The guys who exist on the fringes because they have been rejected by society. I wanted to learn more about this bad boy who lives in the shadows and is more or less disliked by most of the Dark Hunters. As a matter of fact, I eagerly finished this book so I could move onto Zarek's story. All in all, not a bad book at all, but my least favorite in the Dark Hunter series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5136197137699782380" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1448750056" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1448750056" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1448750056?book_show_action=true">Nov 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1448750056" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17201494668540017207">I knew if I hung in there I would start to like this series! This book was a lot of fun. <br/><br/>There is Talon, an ancient Celtic warrior chieftain who is now a Dark Hunter, and Sunshine, a hippy-chick artist who would forget her head if it wasn't attached. I loved Sunny! She is hilarious.<br/><br/>When they meet, Sunny saves Talon after he is run over by a float. Yes, a float. It makes sense when you read it. ;) So, she takes him back to her insanely pink loft and undresses him to wash his clothes while he slee</span>
  <span id="freeText17201494668540017207" style="display:none">I knew if I hung in there I would start to like this series! This book was a lot of fun. <br><br>There is Talon, an ancient Celtic warrior chieftain who is now a Dark Hunter, and Sunshine, a hippy-chick artist who would forget her head if it wasn't attached. I loved Sunny! She is hilarious.<br><br>When they meet, Sunny saves Talon after he is run over by a float. Yes, a float. It makes sense when you read it. ;) So, she takes him back to her insanely pink loft and undresses him to wash his clothes while he sleeps. Of course, she washed his leather pants, and threw them in the dryer. And, then she left his wallet at the laundromat and it was stolen. And, to top it all off, she dropped his car keys and they fell down a drain. So, he wakes up with no pants, money, or the ability to drive his car...not to mention the fact that there is sunlight coming into the windows to fry him.<br><br><b>
  <i>Talon looked uneasily at the woman and the faint sunlight in the room. He wondered which of them was the most lethal to him.</i>
</b><br><br>This starts their adorable courtship. Yes, I said adorable. Sue me!<br><br>I love how Talon finds Sunny charming despite her air-headed ways. And, Sunny herself is hilarious and yet strong in spite of her quirks. She is just what he needs.<br><br>Aside from their story, we get a lot of glimpses into some of the other Dark Hunters and I can't wait to read their stories. Ash - what the hell is his deal? And, Zarek - can't wait for him to get a HEA! Oh, and even Nick, the squire. He is so sarcastic and funny. Love that guy!<br><br>On to the next book!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448262725i/17116759._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

          </span>

How does she make you feel so home with Vampires, Daimons, Were-Wolves, all sorts of Gods, curses, boons, and more importantly it’s like in her world you feel more human! <br/>The best point of the book - <b>Captivatin</b></span>
  <span id="freeText11399541378860562477" style="display:none"><b>Greek Gods</b> + <b>Vampires</b> + <b>Daimons</b> + <b>Were-Wolves</b> + <b>Dark Hunters</b> + <b>Celtic Gods</b> + <b>Insignificant Humans</b> blabbering = the whole book! <br>Concept: <b>2.5/5.0</b><br>Execution: <b>2.5/5.0</b> <br>Characters Bespoken: <b>3.0 /5.0</b><br>Cover: <b>3.0/5.0</b><br>Overall: <b>3.25/5.0</b><br>As for <b>Talon</b> and <b>Sunshine</b>:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1520235016ra/25163616.gif" width="400" height="224" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I am amazed how <b>Sherrilyn Kenyon</b> does it? <div id="review_44132267" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/44132267" />
    <a title="Julianna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/883725-julianna"><img alt="Julianna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442976820p2/883725.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/44132267?book_show_action=true">Jan 23, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Julianna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Julianna" href="/user/show/883725-julianna">Julianna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of PNR Romance, Dark-Hunters, or Sherrilyn Kenyon</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/883725-julianna?shelf=read-2009">read-2009</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/883725-julianna?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer44132267" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16505139775022767983">Reviewed for <a href='http://www.thcreviews.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>THC Reviews</a><br/>"3.5 stars" I know that the <i>Dark-Hunter</i> series is an extremely popular one, and after reading and thoroughly enjoying <i>Fantasy Lover</i>, the prequel, I truly thought that the series would become a favorite of mine too. Unfortunately, I have yet to be completely sucked in by it. The next two stories in the series both suffered from some of the same problems, and for me, <i>Night Embrace</i> has followed in their footsteps. While there were some things that I really liked about the bo</span>
  <span id="freeText16505139775022767983" style="display:none">Reviewed for <a href="http://www.thcreviews.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">THC Reviews</a><br />"3.5 stars" I know that the <i>Dark-Hunter</i> series is an extremely popular one, and after reading and thoroughly enjoying <i>Fantasy Lover</i>, the prequel, I truly thought that the series would become a favorite of mine too. Unfortunately, I have yet to be completely sucked in by it. The next two stories in the series both suffered from some of the same problems, and for me, <i>Night Embrace</i> has followed in their footsteps. While there were some things that I really liked about the book, there are quite a few things that I disliked as well, so I'll start with those. First, there was a huge overabundance of characters, so much so that they stole a lot of face time away from the hero and heroine, and it became difficult to keep track of all of them. To begin with, there are six different classes of beings: deities from Greek and Celtic mythology; daimons (vampires); humans; one ghost; a bunch of demons that were briefly unleashed; and hunters (slayers), of which two different sub-sets, Dark-Hunters and Were-Hunters appear in this story. Then there is the impossibly long list of characters who fall into each of those categories. I literally started jotting down all the ones I knew had appeared in previous Dark-Hunter books or would appear in future books, just so that I could keep them all straight. Here's my quick-reference: Common characters who appear in most of the stories in the series – Acheron, the leader of the Dark-Hunters; Nick Gautier, their main squire or human helper; Selena, another human who has knowledge of the Dark-Hunters; and the Greek goddess, Artemis. Characters from previous Dark-Hunter books – Julian (<i>Fantasy Lover</i>), Kyrian and Amanda (<i>Night Pleasures</i>), and the Greek deities Eros and Psyche who also first appeared in <i>Fantasy Lover</i>. New characters who were introduced in Night Embrace - Zarek (<i>Dance with the Devil</i>), Wulf (<i>Kiss of the Night</i>), Vane and Bride McTierney (<i>Night Play</i>), Valerius (<i>Seize the Night</i>), Wren (<i>Unleash the Night</i>) although he had no dialog, Ravyn (<i>Dark Side of the Moon</i>) although he was only briefly mentioned, and Fang (<i>Bad Moon Rising</i> which will be released in August), plus there was one other Dark-Hunter and a large assortment of Were-Hunters who were either merely mentioned or made very brief appearances, but I'm not aware of them starring in their own books yet. And this wasn't even all the characters, just the ones that appear in other books of the series. Whew! It just seemed like the author thought, “Let's see how many characters I can cram into one book,” and in the end, I thought many of them were very diluted, including Talon and Sunshine who were supposed to be the main characters.<br /><br />My next major issue with <i>Night Embrace</i> is an excess of supernatural powers. Nearly everyone in the book seems to have them, including the humans having mystical psychic powers, which became a bit too much for me to swallow. I think the only prominent “normal” character in the book was Nick. Thus far he does not seem to possess any powers at all which is actually a relief. Again it just seemed like the author tried to cram as many powers into the story as she possibly could, which in my opinion, watered down everyone's powers and made things far too easy. In other paranormal romances I've read, it is only the supernatural creatures who possess abilities, and those are very well defined, usually with base powers that are common to every creature of their race. Then there are a few special ones who have some additional but limited powers. If Dark-Hunters have common powers, I'm having a difficult time identifying them. It seems that so far in this series and especially in this book, Ms. Kenyon makes up powers for the characters as she goes along, and they arbitrarily work or don't work to conform to a given plotline, rather than the plot conforming to the powers that are available. To my way of thinking this is somewhat lazy storytelling, and it is also very confusing to me as the reader, since I have no clear frame of reference as to what any of the characters can do or not do.<br /><br />My last major issue with <i>Night Embrace</i> and the <i>Dark-Hunter</i> series in general is the mythology. I still think that it is rather interesting that Ms. Kenyon decided to base her mythology on real Greek, Celtic and perhaps other myths I'm not aware of. What I dislike though, is that she tends to throw out the names of the various gods and goddesses with little or no mention of who they are. This is all fine and dandy if you've studied mythology, but I haven't since grade school, so once again, trying to keep up can be confusing. Also Ms. Kenyon's own Dark-Hunter mythology is not as well-defined as I would like to see. As she keeps adding new characters to the palette, of course the mythology changes and becomes more complex as well, and in the end, I had just as hard a time remembering all the myths as I did remembering all the characters. No sooner did I think that I had a decent grasp on things than a new myth or character was introduced. I also never had a good feel for the curse placed on Talon by Camulus. As I understood it, anyone Talon loved would die, but Talon's loved ones started dying long before the curse supposedly took effect. I really like to have a good comprehension of the world that an author has created, so feeling like I frequently needed a Dark-Hunter encyclopedia to keep everything straight definitely detracted from my enjoyment of it.<br /><br />As for Talon and Sunshine, the hero and heroine of the book, I can't say that I ever became fully invested from an emotional standpoint in either their individual characters or their relationship. They fall into bed with each other on the first day that they meet (not my favorite way to begin), and their entire relationship develops in a matter of days. Talon and Sunshine share a number of steamy love scenes throughout the story, a couple of which I will admit were rather creative, but without that deep emotional connection, the scenes simply weren't as sensual as I have found in some other romances. They also didn't practice safe sex which is an annoyance to me when there doesn't seem to be any good reason not to. The author relies heavily on the concept of reincarnation to explain the instant attraction the couple has, but it just didn't work for me. Additionally, I'm not a big fan of the push-and-pull conflict in a relationship, and this one definitely had that. First Sunshine acts like her time with Talon was nothing more than a fun fling, and she adamantly has no interest in marriage due to an unhappy first one. Then she comes around in a just a few days only to have Talon be the one who is doing the pushing away, because he is afraid that he will loose her to his curse just like everyone else he ever loved in his mortal life. I really like when characters are able to show their vulnerabilities by sharing their hopes, dreams and life experiences with each other, but Sunshine comes into an awareness of what Talon is and the things he suffered through her own past life memories and her friend Selena's knowledge of the Dark-Hunters. Having things happen this way effectively shut down the lines of communication and consequently suppressed the intimacy of their relationship. As I mentioned before, I felt that Talon and Sunshine were very overshadowed by the other characters and plotlines too. I did like Talon who was a very tortured hero, one of my favorite kinds, and I thought that Sunshine could be very endearing with her sweet scatterbrained ways. I just felt like they were short-changed, and I never really got to know either of them well enough for them to truly stand out to me.<br /><br />Now for some of the things I really liked about <i>Night Embrace</i> that made me give it a few extra points. First, just one word...Acheron. Acheron is almost a larger-than-life character who carried a large part of this story on his very broad shoulders. He literally emanates power and sex appeal right off the pages of the book, and absolutely walks away with every scene he is in. In retrospect, this may not have been such a good thing, but I don't really care. I'm already crazy about him and can't believe I have seventeen more books and novellas to go before I get to his story.:-( The next thing I liked...Zarek. He may have had plenty of moments when he acted like a total jerk, but it was easy to tell that there is much more depth lurking beneath the surface. I for one can't wait to find out more about him, and see this hardened warrior find some peace and happiness. Another thing I enjoyed was the historical flashback sequences with Talon and his first wife Nynia. Although tragic, I found those scenes to be the most romantic in the entire book, and strangely, I felt far more connected to these two as a couple than I did to Talon and Sunshine. Also, I rather enjoyed the testosterone-laced interactions between Acheron, Zarek, Talon and Valerius when they all meet together early in the story. Having that much alpha maleness concentrated in one place was something of a heady brew. Finally, even though there were some minor plot holes and inconsistencies in it, I still really enjoyed the climactic scene of the book, although that's probably because Acheron pretty much took center-stage for it.<br /><br />In addition to my major complaints there were a few other more minor ones as well. I thought there were quite a few passages that were repetitive. The author begins by giving certain parts of Talon's backstory and then filling in the details as the tale progresses, but each time something new was added, there were also things that were reiterated. There were also a few inconsistencies in the details, such as how Talon is able to call Acheron and actually get him one time and Styxx another. I thought that the explanation as to why Talon was allowed to marry Nynia in the past even though she was far beneath him in station was rather weak. There was also mention of Vane being indebted to Ash, but I was left wondering exactly what that debt was. Perhaps this will be explored in a later book. Lastly, Ms. Kenyon tends to throw in new terms specifically related to the world she has created. While it is important that these new words be defined, she always seems to bring the story to a screeching halt while giving the explanation, which is a little annoying. Although, <i>Night Embrace</i> failed to wow me, and the jury is still out on the <i>Dark-Hunter</i> series as a whole, I do plan to continue with it. I was extremely intrigued by Zarek, and his story is the next full-length novel in the series, making me want to read it right away. I'm also so enthralled by Acheron, I don't think I would be able to quit the series at least until I've reached his story. Since <i>Fantasy Lover</i> is still one of my top five all-time favorites, I know that Sherrilyn Kenyon can write a romance with the kind of relationship development I crave, so I'll just have to hope that there will be more books in the <i>Dark-Hunter</i> series that exhibit this type of storytelling. <i>Night Embrace</i> is the second novel in the series. There are currently a total of 19 full-length novels in the <i>Dark-Hunter</i> series and quite a number of related novellas and graphic novels as well, with more still to come. A complete list of all the books and their recommended reading order can be found on Sherrilyn Kenyon's website.<br /><br />*Review updated 9/14/10</span>

  <span id="freeText17933581360352898352" style="display:none">4.5 stars<br /><br />A lot going on in this book. For someone binge reading, it took some adjusting to say this isn't Amanda but Sunshine. I'm giving the next book a try because I like a broken guy. I pray the female lead isn't a whiny southern bell in tone. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10170200559958902061">This reminds of the cover art for Pink Floyd’s Dark Side of the Moon album. While I didn’t love Talon and Sunshine’s story, I can appreciate it for what it is - a solid stepping stone for what is to come!<br/><br/>Prior to this, Kenyon hadn’t included much to build the breadth and depth of the Dark Hunter world. <br/>Enter Night Embrace! Like a good prism spinning light into rainbows (see what I did there?! 🤘 And we’re back to Pink Floyd), the expanded character scape, location scouting and the deeper dive int</span>
  <span id="freeText10170200559958902061" style="display:none">This reminds of the cover art for Pink Floyd’s Dark Side of the Moon album. While I didn’t love Talon and Sunshine’s story, I can appreciate it for what it is - a solid stepping stone for what is to come!<br /><br />Prior to this, Kenyon hadn’t included much to build the breadth and depth of the Dark Hunter world. <br />Enter Night Embrace! Like a good prism spinning light into rainbows (see what I did there?! 🤘 And we’re back to Pink Floyd), the expanded character scape, location scouting and the deeper dive into the mythology is like a melting ice cream cone - you just can’t get to it fast enough! <br /><br />Although, I do have to wonder how we defeat the enemy if we’re constantly losing our DH powers as main characters are introduced? I mean think about it! DH’s don’t grow on trees and with Kenyon being like 40 books into the series, talk about a sucker punch to Artemis’ military organization. Just sayin’!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10170200559958902061" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer300379845" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14744806559343082526"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“So there’s hope?”<br/>“Honey, there’s always hope.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><i>Night Embrace</i> has a perfect and smoothly-built storyline. It is not only a pretty frame story for the romance, but a vibrant, thrilling action line with powerful and serious antagonists, a grandiose conspiracy, mystery, surprising twists, and important and significant secondary characters.<br/><br/>Talon’s backstory is unique, well-developed, and heartbreaking. It is filled with love, revenge, fate, sorrow, intrigue, and myth mixing with history. </span>
  <span id="freeText14744806559343082526" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“So there’s hope?”<br />“Honey, there’s always hope.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><i>Night Embrace</i> has a perfect and smoothly-built storyline. It is not only a pretty frame story for the romance, but a vibrant, thrilling action line with powerful and serious antagonists, a grandiose conspiracy, mystery, surprising twists, and important and significant secondary characters.<br /><br />Talon’s backstory is unique, well-developed, and heartbreaking. It is filled with love, revenge, fate, sorrow, intrigue, and myth mixing with history. It's only a plus that he is stunning inside and out, he is naughty and amusing.<br /><br />Sunshine’s heritage and family is extraordinary. I love her mother, she is so cool!<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I’m not a werewolf.”<br />Starla looked really disappointed by the news. “What a pity. You know, when you live in New Orleans, you expect to meet the undead at least once in a while.” She looked back to Sunshine. “You think we should move? Maybe if we lived over by Anne Rice we might catch sight of a vampire or werewolf.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />In <i>Night Embrace</i> Ms. Kenyon reveals intriguing crumbs of information about the <i>Dark-Hunterverse</i>, about its characters and myth, making you eager to know more about it.<br /><br /><a href="http://exinasreadings.tumblr.com/tagged/Night-Embrace" rel="nofollow noopener">My favorite quotes.</a></span>

<div id="review_1008808892" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1008808892" />
    <a title="Carmen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25353295-carmen"><img alt="Carmen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1412617445p2/25353295.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1008808892?book_show_action=true">Jul 27, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carmen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carmen" href="/user/show/25353295-carmen">Carmen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6586850-night-embrace">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Paranormal Romance Fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25353295-carmen?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25353295-carmen?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25353295-carmen?shelf=traditionally-published">traditionally-published</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25353295-carmen?shelf=she-says">she-says</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25353295-carmen?shelf=published2003">published2003</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1008808892" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1270781174162794619">Talon is a Celt. Born 1,500 years ago, he has a tragic backstory... like all demon-hunters in this series. (I refuse to call them Dark-Hunters... it's just so silly sounding.) ANYWAY. <br/>- At age 7, he and his infant sister Caera were thrown out of their Druid tribe because their parents died.<br/> - They're taken in by their birth clan, the Celts, but are hated and despised because their mother left the clan to marry a Druid.<br/> - Talon has to put the beat down on everyone to gain respect for him and his </span>
  <span id="freeText1270781174162794619" style="display:none">Talon is a Celt. Born 1,500 years ago, he has a tragic backstory... like all demon-hunters in this series. (I refuse to call them Dark-Hunters... it's just so silly sounding.) ANYWAY. <br />- At age 7, he and his infant sister Caera were thrown out of their Druid tribe because their parents died.<br /> - They're taken in by their birth clan, the Celts, but are hated and despised because their mother left the clan to marry a Druid.<br /> - Talon has to put the beat down on everyone to gain respect for him and his sister.<br /> - His uncle, his only semi-ally in the clan, is murdered.<br /> - His aunt is raped and murdered.<br /> - His loving, wonderful wife Nynia dies in childbirth and their son is stillborn.<br /> - The last straw comes in the form of the clan killing his beloved little sister right in front of him.<br /> - Oh, and he's cursed by a god that any mortal he loves will die. <br /><br />He sells his soul for immortality and vengeance and becomes a demon-hunter. Acheron (head ancient demon-hunter) teaches Talon to kill his feelings and be calm and level-headed instead of consumed with rage and grief.<br /><br />All his feelings are dangerously reawakened upon meeting Sunshine Runningwolf in 2003.<br />...<br /><br />THINGS I LIKED:<br /> - Talon is so flippin' patient. There's nothing sexier than a man who has no temper. This is a personal turn-on of mine, and rating romance is really all about whether you agree with the author's idea of sexy or not. Sunshine, especially, needs this kind of guy because she's a flake who forgets stuff, gets distracted, and loses things. He never loses her temper with her or makes her feel bad for being a ditz. <br /><br />- Talon being a carnivorous he-man type and Sunshine being a strong vegetarian, hippie-dippy artist person with a house that is like a pink explosion. It's cute seeing them deal with the "opposite"-ness of each other.<br /><br /> - The "bring-home-the-wounded-dangerous-man-and-heal-him-while-letting-him-sleep-at-your-place" trope. I love this trope and thoroughly enjoy it every time it is wheeled out. Sunshine gets saved by Talon when she's attacked by demons. Then he's hit by a car and she takes him home to tend to his wounds. So cute! A total predictable plot device, but I love it.<br /><br /> - I'm making plans for all side characters in this novel. I am shipping Vane and Bride really hard. I love romance novels with fat heroines and really want Kenyon to write this book about chubby little Bride for me! Then - dark, psychotic, snarling, Zarek - the demon-hunter that everyone fears but we, the readers, see has a secret heart of gold. TOTALLY want to see him get tamed by some sweet, loving woman with infinite patience. I can't wait to see that! Happily dreaming about future pairings was half the fun of this novel. :)<br /><br /> - Sunshine refuses to take orders from Talon or her father. No matter what's going on, she's fierce about protecting her autonomy and independence. I liked it. Usually the heroine gives in because "oh, it's so dangerous" or something, but Sunshine stays strong. She doesn't let the men tell her "it's for your own good" and I really appreciated that. It rarely happens in romance novels.<br /><br /> - Sunshine's kick-butt grandma. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Who turns out to be the goddess Morrigán!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /> - Sunshine's emotions and thoughts regarding <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ herself as Sunshine in this life, and her past self as Nynia in her past life. Does Talon love her for herself? Or does he love her because she's his dead wife reincarnated? Will he expect her to be meek and submissive like Nynia was? Or will he accept that she's strong and independent? Will marriage with him be a form of indentured servitude as it was with her ex-husband Jerry?  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I'm glad these issues are discussed and addressed.<br /><br /> - The fact that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ both Talon and Nynia are virgins when they have sex for the first time as a couple. I'm sick of the men being super-experienced and the females being virginal. Nice equal footing, here.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /> - Sunshine refusing to allow Talon back into her bed until he tells her some pertinent details about himself. <br />...<br /><br />THINGS I DIDN'T LIKE:<br /> - Talon piercing Sunshine's vein and drinking her blood. This is portrayed as a sexual, erotic activity. I think it's disgusting.<br /><br /> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ At the end, both Talon and Sunshine are granted human lives but immortality for no reason that I could see. It's ridiculous and cheesy and unnecessary.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /> - Talon having a little showdown with Sunshine's putz ex-husband. I understand that it's a common female fantasy (your ex shows up and you're with an amazing-looking man who can kick his butt) but it seemed ridiculous and out-of-place in this book. Sometimes it works, and sometimes it doesn't. Here, it didn't.<br /><br /> - The whole Eros subplot. Lame and unnecessary. <br /><br /> - Sex drugs. At one point Sunshine is dosed by the bad guys with a potent sex drug that makes her into a nymphomaniac. The bad guys don't take advantage of her, which I'm grateful for, but I expected Talon to be more of a mensch here. He initially refuses to have sex with her while she's under the influence, but then quickly gives in. I don't like this dubious consent garbage. I'm disappointed in Talon and Kenyon.<br /><br /> - I hate seeing Ash trapped in sexual slavery. I expect Kenyon to deal with this at a later date, but I was hating HATING having to read about poor Ash having to kneel and submit and have sex with that disgusting woman.<br /><br /> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The whole "you're my dead wife reincarnated" trope. I hate this trope. I want people to fall in love for who they are - not who they WERE. Although it is handled more delicately and with more thoughtfulness in this book than I've seen in the past - I'm still not a fan of this plot device.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /> - I didn't understand the "emotions are key to Talon's powers" crap AT ALL. I can't even say I disliked it because I didn't comprehend it enough to like it or not. Kenyon didn't do a good job at explaining what was going on here. Fail.<br /><br /> - OMG. The objectification of men in this book is just disgusting. Sunshine strips Talon's unconscious body. When he wakes up, both she and her mom talk about him and his naked body as if he weren't even in the room, making complimentary remarks on the size of his penis, etc. Her mom unilaterally decides to call him "Steve" - without even asking what his name is - as if he's a stray dog that her daughter brought home and they get to name and claim as their own. IT'S NOT OKAY. It's supposed to be cute and funny - after all, what threat are these women to him? He could kill them with a flick of his wrist, etc. but I am not amused. It's not right, and it's definitely not "cute." This happens often. Sunshine frequently looks at and appraises Talon's body as if it's a flippin' piece of art and not a living, breathing human being. No me gusta. And after Sunshine and Talon have sex, Sunshine immediately gives her best friend all the intimate details. Am I the only one left who thinks that what you do in the bedroom with your boo is private? Geez Louise. Sunshine was not winning any points with me!<br />...<br /><br />Overall, a fun book, but still not Kenyon's best. Close, we're getting closer...<br /><br />3 REAL STARS, 4 ROMANCE STARS</span>
  <a data-text-id="1270781174162794619" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="WhiskeyintheJar" class="user" itemprop="url" name="WhiskeyintheJar" href="/user/show/2763722-whiskeyinthejar">WhiskeyintheJar</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2763722-whiskeyinthejar?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1145745710" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7324614766075022396"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380347446ra/701813.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>This is the best way I can describe how I felt reading this book. I didn't read the previous books in the series, so I'm definitely at fault for feeling a little behind and lost but holy guacamole. I liked the book but trying to grasp all the characters, their identities, and all their agendas made me sweat from exhaustion.<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437931370ra/15647513.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>How I imagine the author writing this. Seriously, we've got gods from EVERY mythology, paranormal beings, and bears, oh my! You know someone out there has cataloged all these </span>
  <span id="freeText7324614766075022396" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380347446ra/701813.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This is the best way I can describe how I felt reading this book. I didn't read the previous books in the series, so I'm definitely at fault for feeling a little behind and lost but holy guacamole. I liked the book but trying to grasp all the characters, their identities, and all their agendas made me sweat from exhaustion.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437931370ra/15647513.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>How I imagine the author writing this. Seriously, we've got gods from EVERY mythology, paranormal beings, and bears, oh my! You know someone out there has cataloged all these characters, their connections, and biography; bless their heart.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437931370ra/15647514.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>If there was a visual of me reading this. Look, this book has been out a while and others have written amazing reviews for it, I'm not going to even attempt one. This is just all about my narcissistic need to put my feelings out there. Even with the massive amount of characters and story lines (the writing gets a little loose at times), I felt the need to hang on for the ride. There is a certain charm to characters and writing (the hero of this book, Talon, is also too hot to trot with his Celtic tattoos and general hero-ness) that kept me locked in. Our leads have the whole soulmate thing going on, so no gradual falling in love but kind of instant, they also got ignored more than I liked in favor of the overall story arcs. <br> <br>I'll definitely be continuing with the series (so, there's like a dragon inside Acheron?!) and I guess just hope as more heroes/heroines get their individual stories, the books won't be as jammed packed and things will make more sense.<br>Or maybe I'm in for more of,<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437931370ra/15647515.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Either way, sign me up! <br>If you've read the series, discuss your feels and let me know if things improve/fall apart.<br> <br>Thanks to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/3709091-lover-of-romance" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover of Romance</a> for the rec!</span>

<div id="review_2598520533" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2598520533" />
    <a title="Alaina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/50620706-alaina"><img alt="Alaina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451325817p2/50620706.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2598520533?book_show_action=true">Nov 28, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alaina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alaina" href="/user/show/50620706-alaina">Alaina</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50620706-alaina?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2598520533" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5316043114769656482">UGH!<br/><br/>Okay this book and possibly the series - is just meh. I can't decide if it's the characters, the accents, the narrator, or the entire story that just nudges me wrong. Somehow I always end up annoyed while listening to them. It took me a couple of days to finish this book because of any of those reasons mentioned above.<br/><br/><i>Night Embrace</i> is the second installment of the <i>Dark-Hunter</i> series. I still think the way these guys become a dark hunter is interesting.. but that's pretty much it. The girls i</span>
  <span id="freeText5316043114769656482" style="display:none">UGH!<br /><br />Okay this book and possibly the series - is just meh. I can't decide if it's the characters, the accents, the narrator, or the entire story that just nudges me wrong. Somehow I always end up annoyed while listening to them. It took me a couple of days to finish this book because of any of those reasons mentioned above.<br /><br /><i>Night Embrace</i> is the second installment of the <i>Dark-Hunter</i> series. I still think the way these guys become a dark hunter is interesting.. but that's pretty much it. The girls in this series just end up annoying me somehow. Also, her name was sunshine.. and that just irked me every time it was mentioned,<br /><br />Other than her, there's Talon and he was just okay. I honestly didn't really care about their relationship of what would happen to them. I did like that she could possibly be his dead wife reincarnated.. but after a while, I kind of just gave up on them. <br /><br />Overall, I wanted this over and once it was.. I rejoiced with some wine. No idea when I will dive into the next book.. but I'll be hoping that it's a lot better than the first two!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2634739160" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6954265595343366478">I had read the first book "Dark Pleasures" in the "Dark Hunter" series like years ago, but i still remember Talon appearing naked in the first book if i am not mistaked,and i remember strongly liking this blonde sexually character and reading about his story in "Night Embrace" is a pleasure i can`t deny. He is the goldenhearted badboy i wish for myself and his romance with the half-crazy and bold Sunsine undid me...they are so beautiful and sexy together..just YUM!<br/><br/>Sherrilyn Kenyon knows her genr</span>
  <span id="freeText6954265595343366478" style="display:none">I had read the first book "Dark Pleasures" in the "Dark Hunter" series like years ago, but i still remember Talon appearing naked in the first book if i am not mistaked,and i remember strongly liking this blonde sexually character and reading about his story in "Night Embrace" is a pleasure i can`t deny. He is the goldenhearted badboy i wish for myself and his romance with the half-crazy and bold Sunsine undid me...they are so beautiful and sexy together..just YUM!<br /><br />Sherrilyn Kenyon knows her genre and she writes it with such a flow and presents characters that you can`t wait to explore. It was interesting that Sunshine is a reincarnated version of Talon`s wife Nynia who died..and that while having the same souls they aren`t the same person. And watching Talon falling in love all over again in his soulmate was heavenly to watch.He never could let go of her, and it all was so painful to watch when the whole world was against them. Even then these two stubbornly fought for their love and that was so epic that i felt everything they felt together. Sunshine with her honesty and humor made me laugh out many times, and how her sex-drive matched with Talon`s was so HOT HOT DOUBLE HOT! These two could make love a whole night without ever having enough, damn how perfect they are for each other..and how i love them! The painful emotions of rage and sadness Talon had buried inside himself all the time being a Hunter, he undid me with his great, lonely but oh so beautiful heart that when Sunshine heals him that i nearly cried of joy for him.He had suffered so much in his life that losing Sunshine would have killed him,that much was clear.So he of all deserved happiness with Sunshine the most, and i am so glad for him.<br /><br />The enemies that are in fact twins, Styxx and Acheron are highly intriguing and i know that they are the very favourite characters of many fans of this series, and i so look forward to reading their stories in "Acheron" and "Styxx". Zarek and Valerius are said to be half-brothers and i especially look forward to reading the brooding Zarek`s book, he seems so lonely that its gut-wrenching to read from his POV. And Nick was so funny that i instantly liked him, i also know that he has his own series. Oh i knew there would be something between Bride and Vane, the way he was looking at her, KYAA and they have their story in "Night Play" which i find exciting! Damn awesome book overall, with fantasy, excitement, humor and irresistible warriors that made me drool...and best of all: the all-consuming, lustful and eternal love-story between the bright Sunshine and the one man who would give up his life for her without a thought, the fearless warrior Talon.!</span>
  <a data-text-id="6954265595343366478" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_47447008" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/47447008" />
    <a title="Nichole (DirrtyH)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/74998-nichole-dirrtyh"><img alt="Nichole (DirrtyH)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1365696753p2/74998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/47447008?book_show_action=true">Feb 24, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nichole (DirrtyH)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nichole (DirrtyH)" href="/user/show/74998-nichole-dirrtyh">Nichole (DirrtyH)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780312984823" href="/book/show/84140.Night_Embrace">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74998-nichole-dirrtyh?shelf=abandoned">abandoned</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer47447008" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10765542555517027140">Man, oh man, did I try. I really, really did. I swear. But I'm just not ever going to finish this book.<br/><br/>So here's what I don't like about these books. It took me awhile to put my finger on it, but here's the bottom line. Come close so I can whisper it in your ear. Ready?<br/><br/><b>
  <i>Sherrilyn Kenyon is a big dork.</i>
</b><br/><br/>That's right, I said it. She's trying to write (presumbly edgy) books about big, bad warriors in leather but she can't get the dialogue right because she's a big dork! No one has used the term "n</span>
  <span id="freeText10765542555517027140" style="display:none">Man, oh man, did I try. I really, really did. I swear. But I'm just not ever going to finish this book.<br /><br />So here's what I don't like about these books. It took me awhile to put my finger on it, but here's the bottom line. Come close so I can whisper it in your ear. Ready?<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Sherrilyn Kenyon is a big dork.</i>
</b><br /><br />That's right, I said it. She's trying to write (presumbly edgy) books about big, bad warriors in leather but she can't get the dialogue right because she's a big dork! No one has used the term "not" since 1991. (You know as in "Yeah, that'll happen - not!" Nope, not since 1991, and even then only 8 year old kids said it. This is only the most readily available example of lame dialogue - it certainly is not the only one. Kenyon is a dork which makes all of the characters in her books dorks. I like sharp dialogue, sue me.<br /><br />The other big problem is that she has no sense of subtlety when it comes to the attraction between the hero and heroine. She likes to beat the reader over the head with it. Okay, I get it already! They're hot for each other. How about some story? Please?! <br /><br />This particular book has some other weaknesses - namely that the plot is so deeply hidden behind all the sex and attraction and introduction of a myriad of new characters whose only purpose is to give her another hero for the next book that I simply got exhausted and gave up. I'm sure Talon found some way to get around his curse and they lived happily ever after. I just don't care how anymore. I'm done.<br /><br />The only good thing about this book is what was good about the two that came before it, and presumably what will be good about the subsequent ones, and that is Talon's story.<br />The whole series is built around the premise of warriors who are only warriors because they suffered a great betrayal, and so far they all have really compelling betrayal stories. I liked reading about Talon's past.<br /><br />And okay, both Talon and Sunshine are pretty likeable, but they're just not compelling in the way I need them to be.<br /><br />So that's it. No more Dark Hunters for me. Sorry, guys.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10765542555517027140" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText11323416206492660447" style="display:none">Rating 4.5<br /><br />This is Talons story and my oh my was it hot! I am not sure where to even begin, I guess I will keep this review short and sweet and just say that Kenyon has done a fantastic job with her characters. Sunshine was so laugh out loud funny! Her eccentricities never became too much, she was just warm and very believeable. I really like all the additional information we get throughout the story as well. I have to say that I am really liking this new world that Kenyon has created. Her characters are all made of awesome and if you have read my other reviews of the past two books then you know that I am definitely a fangirl.         <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer3209959098&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3209959098" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18199996849564008857">This series is filled with so much wonder! Based in the good ole magical place called New Orleans there are psychics, shifters (that you have and have never even heard of), vampires, dark hunters, were-hunters, daimons, gods, goddesses etc. The list goes on (I am serious lol). It is literally a supernatural mash with some things you have heard of and many you have not. The world built is so vibrant and colorful and keeps you guessing, wondering what will happen next. Each supernatural has abilit</span>
  <span id="freeText18199996849564008857" style="display:none">This series is filled with so much wonder! Based in the good ole magical place called New Orleans there are psychics, shifters (that you have and have never even heard of), vampires, dark hunters, were-hunters, daimons, gods, goddesses etc. The list goes on (I am serious lol). It is literally a supernatural mash with some things you have heard of and many you have not. The world built is so vibrant and colorful and keeps you guessing, wondering what will happen next. Each supernatural has abilities that you could have never imagined and then more come along with even cooler abilities or even hidden abilities you never knew they had all along throughout the story. It is amazing! This book was focused on Talon and Sunshine. Sunshine is witty, HILARIOUS (I am not kidding I could not stop laughing with her) bold, confident, artistic, curvy, and truly outspoken! Talon is so beautiful and sexy and sexual omg! So serious! Sunshine and Talon have the best sex and chemistry and sexual chemistry ugh wait until you read the love scenes. *Phew* Is it hot in here? Haha! I loved every bit of it! Outside of the sexy sexy Talon is a warrior with a past that will make your heart ache. Any person before becoming a dark hunter has something so tragic happen to them that their cries reach Artemis (the goddess) and she gives them a choice. If one chooses to be a dark hunter they are given the opportunity to take vengeance on those who betrayed them, receive powers of their own, and become immortal. In return they must swear fealty to Artemis, bury their pain somehow to pursue their missions without being clouded or distracted, and protect the human race from daimons. The only problem is in order to bury the past it has to stay buried but when Talon meets Sunshine he can't keep anything hidden, he can't control his emotions and everything is coming back to him. He can't deny who she is or the passions and emotions she has awakened in him. He can't stay away from her but in order to truly protect her he feels like he has to...if only that were possible. When a dark hunter meets his mate that means it is time to face your demons and win back your soul so that you can truly be with your soulmate. When two people are soulmates, nobody, not even a God or Goddess can keep them from one another. One thing is for certain, Talon and Sunshine were made for eachother ❤</span>
  <a data-text-id="18199996849564008857" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780312984823" href="/book/show/84140.Night_Embrace">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer129439653" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9081607354874248573"><b>Posted on<a href='http://underthecoversbookblog.blogspot.ca/2012/04/review-night-embrace-by-sherrilyn.html' rel='nofollow noopener'> Under the Covers</a></b><br/><br/> <b>Dear Talon,<br/> I’ll hold your spear.<br/> Love,<br/> Ann</b><br/><br/><br/>NIGHT EMBRACE is the second book in the Dark Hunters series and I have to say that it is definitely my favorite so far! I usually have a problem with Kenyon’s tendency to overdramaticize, but for this book, I don’t think she pulled anything crazy or over the top.<br/><br/>As always, the hero is a tortured soul. Talon has lost something that he holds dear. But he doesn’t allow it to run his life now. I loved Talon’s lighthearted attitude</span>
  <span id="freeText9081607354874248573" style="display:none"><b>Posted on<a href="http://underthecoversbookblog.blogspot.ca/2012/04/review-night-embrace-by-sherrilyn.html" rel="nofollow noopener"> Under the Covers</a></b><br /><br /> <b>Dear Talon,<br /> I’ll hold your spear.<br /> Love,<br /> Ann</b><br /><br /><br />NIGHT EMBRACE is the second book in the Dark Hunters series and I have to say that it is definitely my favorite so far! I usually have a problem with Kenyon’s tendency to overdramaticize, but for this book, I don’t think she pulled anything crazy or over the top.<br /><br />As always, the hero is a tortured soul. Talon has lost something that he holds dear. But he doesn’t allow it to run his life now. I loved Talon’s lighthearted attitude. He was fun, flirty and soo damn sexy. The first part of this book has lots of sex in it (not that I’m complaining) so Kenyon really established Talon as the ultimate sex warrior. She even comes up with some very interesting positions. I’ll make note of those, thank you very much.<br /><br />Another great thing about this series is Sunshine. She really sparkled in this book. I loved her quirky ways and her unique spirit. She compliments Talon well and I loved that they were so willing to give up their world for each other.<br /><br />With a strong romance and an even stronger camaraderie between the Dark Hunters, I can say I’m very excited to see what’s in store for Zarek!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9081607354874248573" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Filled with laughter and friendship, Sunshine leads the sweet life of an artist. Drowning in pink and purple flowers while singing Puff the Magic Dragon, she is everything that will drive Talon up the wall. Or seduce him with amusement.<br/> <br/><i>“You know, Sunshine, you need to find a man like that to marry. Someone so well hung that even after three or four kids, he’d still be wall to wall.”<br/> <br/>Talon</i></span>
  <span id="freeText13127147731066003364" style="display:none">Night Embrace is the amazing story of Talon and Sunshine.<br /> <br />Sunshine comes from a carefree and loving family. Filled with laughter and friendship, Sunshine leads the sweet life of an artist. Drowning in pink and purple flowers while singing Puff the Magic Dragon, she is everything that will drive Talon up the wall. Or seduce him with amusement.<br /> <br /><i>“You know, Sunshine, you need to find a man like that to marry. Someone so well hung that even after three or four kids, he’d still be wall to wall.”<br /> <br />Talon gaped. Sunshine laughed.</i><br /> <br />Talon, another Dark-Hunter with a tragic past, protects humans through the centuries of loneliness. Calm and collected, he has one mission in life. Protect and survive. Forcing the emotions and pain of betrayal, he glides along the way through the days, years and centuries without mourning the loss of his wife, his son and his family.<br /> <br /><i>“Never let anyone know you. Never give them a chance to realize you don’t age. Move through the darkness ever watchful, ever alert. We are all that stands between the humans and slavery. Without us, they all die and their souls are lost forever. Our responsibilities are great. Our battles numerous and legendary. But at the end of the night, you go home alone where no one knows what it is you have done to save the world that fears you. You can never bask in your glory. You can never know love or family. We are Dark-Hunters. We are forever powerful. We are forever alone.”</i><br /> <br />Acheron becomes more engrossed in this book. Kenyon gives you a few glances into his past that will leave you frustrated with curiosity. No worries! His novel will be read before you know it!<br /> <br />Fighting their love for one another, Talon and Sunshine are soul mates. Reincarnated with Talon’s wife’s soul, they are extremely attracted and are unable to keep their hands to themselves <br /><br />This book is far more sexual than Night Pleasures or Fantasy Lover.<br /> <br />Many characters are introduced in this book. I love most of them and I look forward to rereading their stories!<br /> <br />Vane and Fang, wolves who can take human form, repay a debt to Acheron and form a temporary alliance. With this, the book unravels many stories to come. This book is a MUST read if you plan on continuing with the other books in this series.<br /> <br />I recommend this book to mature adults only. Although this book is filled with paranormal yumminess, I highly advise against allowing a teenager or child to read this series. People tend to forget that children are indeed children and NOT young adults. This book is not for innocent eyes.<br /> <br />Extremely delectable sexual and violent content.<br /> <br />Line of the book:<br /> <br /><i>“But without pain, you can’t have joy. It’s the balance that makes us appreciate the extremes.”<br /></i></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_155131079" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/155131079" />
    <a title="Arlene" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1746727-arlene"><img alt="Arlene" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1347048609p2/1746727.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/155131079?book_show_action=true">Mar 18, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Arlene" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Arlene" href="/user/show/1746727-arlene">Arlene</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780312984823" href="/book/show/84140.Night_Embrace">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=read-2011">read-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=greek-mythology">greek-mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer155131079" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6295488405546623934"><i>He who lets fear rule him, has fear for a master.</i><br/><br/><b>Night Embrace</b> is the third installment I’ve read in the Dark Hunter series. It’s fun, fast paced and filled with exciting characters. I will admit after reading three books in this series that it’s starting to remind me of JR Ward’s BDB series with eternal creatures that roam the night protecting humans from vampire baddies. Their ultimate leader is a fearless woman, their demise will lead them to Shadedom… yes, quite a bit of similarities coupled</span>
  <span id="freeText6295488405546623934" style="display:none"><i>He who lets fear rule him, has fear for a master.</i><br /><br /><b>Night Embrace</b> is the third installment I’ve read in the Dark Hunter series. It’s fun, fast paced and filled with exciting characters. I will admit after reading three books in this series that it’s starting to remind me of JR Ward’s BDB series with eternal creatures that roam the night protecting humans from vampire baddies. Their ultimate leader is a fearless woman, their demise will lead them to Shadedom… yes, quite a bit of similarities coupled with predictable events that for some reason keeps me entertained and sort of hooked.<br /><br />In <b>Night Embrace</b> we meet Talon and Sunshine (yes, I giggled too when I read her name). Talon has spent the last fifteen hundred years standing between mankind and those who would see them destroyed. He is a Guardian, a Soulless Keeper, neither human, nor Apollite. He exists between the realm of the living and beyond the realm of the dead. As a Dark Hunter, he is eternal unless he finds that one pure heart who will never betray him and free him from his bond to Acheron and Artemis.<br /><br />I really enjoyed the characters. They are strong and actually quite funny. Some of the stuff that comes out of their mouth actually had me laughing out loud in humorous disbelief. There were a few steamy scenes that had me wondering… is that really possible without getting hurt or burning your leg on the exhaust pipe? Really?? But overall, I have no real complaints. I liked it, what can I say??<br /><br />All in all, it was fun and exciting. I’ll keep reading these as I like the mythology, the back-story of the Dark Hunters and I’m curious about a few of the characters and their ultimate fate including Vane and Ceara. Good installment to this series!</span>
  <a data-text-id="6295488405546623934" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vS8u1uqx9oyifbrCGeQsCIusGfFpIGNbZwrQv410+rSuvo+/f5lbytZMBIsv9ufbhAPu6FX3PwqBv5GFMIGtyw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('plqYaQlHyqF8LaoB2w+hy06mD4bof+5DZNGA3MytbX21yzkAnG9n5wgcFEjtHWoYQQn4n9SoshKCZMHmcVg6Ag==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText16582849304955518631" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.mysherrilyn.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Author site</a><br /><a href="http://crynevermore.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Nevermore site</a><br /><a href="http://www.deadmanscross.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Deadman's Cross site</a><br /><a href="http://www.sherrilynkenyon.com/book-series/chronicles-of-nick/" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Chronicles of Nick site</a><br /><a href="http://silentswans.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Silent Swans site</a><br /><a href="http://hunterlegends.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Hunter Legends site</a><br /><a href="http://witchofendor.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Witch of Endor site</a><br /><a href="http://Lordsofavalon.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Lords of Avalon site</a><br /><a href="http://www.facebook.com/AuthorSherrilynKenyon" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Facebook site</a><br /><br />New York Times and international bestselling author Sherrilyn Kenyon is a regular at the #1 spot. With legions of fans known as Paladins (thousands of whom proudly sport tattoos from her series and who travel from all over the world to attend her appearances), her books are always snatched up as soon as they appear on store shelves. Since 2004, she had placed more than 80 novels on the New York Times list in all formats including manga and graphic novels. Her current series are: Dark-Hunters, Chronicles of Nick and The League, and her books are available in over 100 countries where eager fans impatiently wait for the next release.
